Amateur Dramatic Club Mime 177

Performing Today and Tomorrow and Five Days of the New Year

The Shanghai Amateur Dramatic Club is scheduled to present a mime performance at the Lyceum Theatre on the 28th and 29th of this month and from January 1st to 5th next year. The play is titled "Dick Whittington and His Cat," which is an English fairy tale. Mime is rarely performed in Shanghai. Each character in the play does not speak a word, relying entirely on gestures and facial expressions. Even when they speak occasionally, it is very rare. This play is a famous children's myth, and its plot is about the struggle between demons from the lower realm and the fairy queen. The result is that virtue triumphs over evil. Dick Whittington is a poor boy who owns a cat. The cat possesses supernatural powers that bring its owner all kinds of happiness, eventually making him the Mayor of London. He then meets a wealthy merchant's daughter named Alice, and they fall in love and become a couple. Initially, Dick has the blessing of the fairy queen, while the demon tries to destroy him. Later, Dick takes his cat to the East. The demon causes his ship to sink in the sea. Dick then takes refuge on a rocky beach and is captured by the Arabs. The Arab royal palace is suffering from a rat infestation. Every meal is eaten by the rats, and the people in the palace are starving. There is no way to get rid of them. Dick's cat then uses its supernatural powers to capture and kill the rat king. The rat king is a friend of the demon. The Arab king is overjoyed and gives Dick a huge bag of gold. Dick then divides the gold to give it to his fellow travelers. The play is full of interesting interjections, and the scenery of the royal palace is particularly magnificent. There are also pleasing dances. Tickets are sold at Moutrie & Co. on No. 20 Nanjing Road, with prices of four yuan, three yuan, and two yuan. Half price for children for matinees.

Liu Jinfan, Shi Xiangzhou were alternate supervisory committee members. They were immediately sworn in. Next, there was a discussion about a letter from Mr. Zhang Yimi, stating that he could not serve as chairman of this session. It was resolved to reply to the letter, and after unanimous election, it was requested that he try his best to make it difficult. The ceremony was adjourned.

This has also helped the YMCA a lot. It is also said that Sichuan is a vast and resource-rich province, with wealth leading the country. Chunqiu

Little West Heaven 194

— By Zhang Henshui

Chapter 7: Veiling Tears, Selling Oneself into Misery; Paying Attention, Peeking at Invitations, Relying on Sincere Affection

Li Shilian saw cigarettes on the table, conveniently took one, and started smoking. At this moment, an unnatural smile spread across his face as he said to Jia Duocai: "Brother Duocai, we are good friends after all. When I am in absolutely impossible circumstances, you can't possibly not lend me a hand. I was originally thinking that finding a job in the South is always a case of too many monks and too little porridge, making it impossible to get a good position. Places like the Northwest, people don't come, so I took the risk and ran here.

I didn't expect that after arriving here, I realized everyone thinks the same way, and there are quite a few people waiting for vacancies here too. If I go back, I came with fanfare before, and I would feel like I would lose face. But if I want to find a job, I don't know when I can squeeze to the front, truly making it difficult to advance or retreat. Now is the period for developing the Northwest, and the Construction Department needs the most people. Since you know Director Gao, can you help me find a way out?" Jia Duocai said: "Your goal is very big! I'm afraid my position is not sufficient to recommend you, right?" Li Shilian held the cigarette, constantly flicking the ash, while his other hand patted his hair and stroked his chin, laughing: "I don't care about the title. Whatever it is, if I can work for a year or half a year, and resolve my current living situation, that would be enough. For example, let's talk about cars. Now the highway administration should have an Automobile Management Bureau." Jia Duocai said: "You want to be the director of the bureau?" Li Shilian laughed: "How could that be possible? If I can get a branch bureau under the director, that would be more than satisfactory!" Jia Duocai said: "Managing cars, naturally, involves things like transporting goods and passengers. Have you done that before?" Li Shilian shrugged his shoulders twice and laughed: "That doesn't mean only people who have done it before can do it. Who graduated from Jiaotong University and became the Minister of Railways? Who graduated from agricultural university and became the Minister of Industry? If officials and staff had to have done it and studied it before they could do it, there would be a talent crisis. I have been involved in taxation, in various capacities, for three or four years, and I have never studied any finance or economics." (101)

Trivial Football Talk 195

— By Yang Yusheng

Although the winter weather is cold, it doesn't cool down the hearts of football fans! As long as there's an exciting enough football match, the area around the field is still crowded and lively!

I think this is a good phenomenon. We dare not say the kind of "official" words like "promote sports" - actually, there's no need to say them - but compared to dance halls, dog racing tracks, and jai alai courts, although they are all entertainment, football's character is much more elegant!

The money and time I've spent on "watching football" add up to a considerable amount, so I've also earned the nickname "football fan."

During the prime of Lehua, one Saturday afternoon, I was denied leave to watch a game, so I secretly sneaked away to Shen Garden, preferring to enjoy the game to the fullest and face my superior's scolding when I returned, rather than dutifully and obediently be like an ant on a hot pot in the office!

Speaking of Lehua, it fills me with admiration mixed with endless sighs. Perhaps because of the saying, "The world's affairs, after a long period of unity, must divide!" Lehua broke up a long time ago! Luckily, Donghua took over, otherwise we football fans would have died of withdrawal.

In terms of "skill," Donghua is not necessarily inferior to Lehua; but Lehua was "tougher" than Donghua. The reason Lehua could not be called a "complete" team was because it never had enough qualified "wing" players. Donghua has "wings," but only has "skill" and lacks "toughness." Both are lacking!

The psychology of general football fans seems to be consistent "externally"! Most hope to win a few more games against foreigners. If Chinese players can make a few more "hurdles" and make foreigners trip and fall, it's worth clapping and laughing about. But "internally," there are many different factions! Some support Donghua, others support Youyou. Take the matches between Donghua and Youyou in the "Western League" this season, the situation among the spectators is much more tense than among the players competing on the field! I think shouting "good" to cheer on the players is acceptable; but when the players on both sides show signs of being overly aggressive, the spectators shout "fight!" as if they won't be happy unless they see a "wrestling match" in addition to the football game. Isn't that strange?

Snippets 196

— (Shen Shou Ruo)

In the past, people's methods of suppressing talent were merely passive resistance; the so-called "high-brow songs find few singers" is one example.

The methods of suppressing talent used by people today are much harsher! Not only will they not sing along with your high-brow songs, but they will also destroy your melodies to their heart's content.

Warm Hall Evening Meal 197

— Shen Yu

In my hometown's customs, on the wedding night, after the bride and groom perform the ancestral worship ceremony, there is always a "warm hall evening meal."

Naturally, this is a humorous scene. When this humorous scene is about to unfold, it is usually some witty friends, squeezed into the bridal chamber already full of women and children, who tease the bride and groom without restraint, and strongly demand that the groom take the bride's hand and go to the main hall to eat the "warm hall evening meal." Thus, men and women, rustic and pretty, all crowd around the "beautiful couple" towards the main hall.

At this time, in the center of the main hall, two cedar tables have already been placed side by side. On these tables are eight exquisite dishes. After the "beautiful couple" sit down on the two large chairs facing south, the remaining seats are taken by some witty friends.

Thus, the "warm hall evening meal" begins.

First, the guest closest to the groom stands up to pour a cup of wine for the bride and groom, then uses chopsticks to offer this dish and that dish to the groom; but sometimes the groom often declines and does not "appreciate" the offer, so the person offering has to come up with a way to get the groom to eat it.

Gradually, it proceeds to the second person, the third person, ... until everyone sitting around has had their turn, and then the "warm hall evening meal" is over.

However, the time from beginning to end is often extended to three or four hours, because each guest sitting around has to come up with a method – something that will make the bride and groom feel shy and have enough to remember – and ask the bride and groom to do it this way; if not, they are willing to hold on for a long time, until it is done.

The above is a general sketch of the "warm hall evening meal," a custom in my hometown.

Records of Fleeting Fragrance from the Imperial Incense 198

— Originally written by Princess Der Ling of the Qing Dynasty, translated by Qin Shouou

Sometimes, perhaps these medicines happen to be somewhat effective against the patient's illness. Coupled with the patient's own psychological effect, it is easy to see results. After such occasional effectiveness a few times, people attribute most of the ineffectiveness to fate, believing that the great immortal is truly extraordinary.

Even the Empress Dowager, a female politician managing countless affairs every day, honestly has a very stubborn belief in this; but as for me, before I have obtained sufficient evidence, I really dare not believe it blindly.

"Let's just make a hypothetical assumption, Empress Dowager," I suddenly said, struck by a fit of foolishness, forgetting all my inhibitions: "Suppose that the immortal prescription has been obtained, and the medicine has been prepared, and given to"

"The patient has drunk it: but these medicines are really not suitable for the patient's illness, for example, using hot medicine for a heat disease, and cold medicine for a cold disease, wouldn't this be very dangerous for the patient? What if it causes a major disaster?"

The Empress Dowager usually gets angry easily with others, but she treats me with special favor, never with harsh words or stern expressions, always especially tolerant; at this time, after hearing me raise such a strange (actually very reasonable) question, she couldn't help but become very angry.

"How dare you talk such nonsense!" Her face reddened, and she scolded me loudly.

I immediately regretted it too. Although my intention was right, how could I casually criticize the things that the Empress Dowager believed in? We should only blindly obey her like children obey their parents, without any doubts, and I dared to openly express my disagreement to her, which was obviously extremely audacious; if she was unhappy, she could impose any punishment on me. When I thought of this, I couldn't help but feel panicked. (211)

Old Goods Peddler 199

— Han Yu

The old goods peddlers in Shanghai are like the drummers in Beiping, they both buy broken and old things. The only difference is that the drummers beat drums, while they shout out loud.

People who live in Shanghai cannot help but feel the expensiveness of rent. In order to save money, they have to live in extremely small houses. Those useless wastes, like newspapers and old bottles and cans, it feels wasteful to throw away, but there is no place to put them if they are kept. Old goods peddlers buy these kinds of things. Others don't want them, but they are willing to buy them, so they can buy these things at extremely low prices.

The origin of old goods peddlers is probably like this. But later, their business gradually expanded. Of course, some useless old things are bought by them. When in financial difficulties, carrying things to a pawnshop is not very elegant after all, and there are many things that pawnshops are unwilling to accept, so they are sold to old goods peddlers. Fortunately, when selling to them, others will not pay attention, and the old goods peddlers will try their best to deal with such business, not wanting to lose this good deal. If one person's financial resources are insufficient, they will unite several people to buy together.

Old goods peddlers have an association. After they buy things, they transform them themselves. They make old things into new ones, repair broken things, and then take these things to the association to sell. There, there are many regular customers, who specialize in buying old things.

I am a book addict, and I also wander around the old goods association in my spare time, getting one or two books that I need. But sometimes there are also very unexpected discoveries, like being able to buy many complete sets of magazines by accident.

Whether buying or selling, negotiating prices with old goods peddlers is an extremely troublesome matter. When buying, they will point out many shortcomings of that thing, making it a pretext for reducing the price. But when selling, they can point out many advantages, so they can raise the price. But they rarely have arrogant tempers, and within the possible range, a deal can always be made.

Social Snapshot

Unemployed Rich People 200

— Zhang Zhenlu

People often say, "Shanghai is paved with gold, just waiting for people to bend down and pick it up." People from rural towns and villages are transported to Shanghai in large numbers, seduced by this rumor, wanting to realize their golden dream; as a result, the streets are only filled with a few more vagrants, and the newspapers have a few more stories of kidnapping and trafficking! Although, in this city of endless wonders, there are indeed many people who have neither permanent property nor permanent employment, but can sit and eat in peace, living comfortably, like the people I want to describe. I admire them for having the richness of the rich, so I affectionately call them "Unemployed Rich People."

One year, my family moved to a certain neighborhood. Every night, I heard the sounds of mahjong games and radios from next door, which greatly interfered with my writing work, so I could only dare to be angry but not dare to speak. "Harmony is the most valuable, the way of the former kings," this is not me being good at reading broken sentences, it is really the legacy of the sages, too suitable for worldly affairs and human relationships! But look, the Sister Sun from next door, after talking to my wife a few times, gradually became acquainted; even I soon got to know the so-called Mr. Sun, and was even sometimes invited to join the mahjong game. So I had to endure the hidden pain and uphold the virtue of neighborly harmony. However, I learned about their family's living situation because of this, which can be considered compensation for the damage.

Their family rented two adjacent single-family shikumen houses, spent some renovation costs, and sublet the houses to others, so sixteen families lived in the two houses! This residential area has a very economical distribution method, which can be used for subletting to each household, now publicly announce that each house is divided as follows: the living room and patio, with a glass canopy built on the patio, is for one household, a small room is blocked off behind the living room for one household, a mezzanine is built on it, and steps are used to go in and out halfway, for one household, the front building for one household, the rear building for one household, the attic for one household, the kitchen room - commonly known as the pavilion room - for one household, and its roof was originally a drying platform, which is built into a wooden house for one household. The kitchen is shared. The head of the stairs and outside the upstairs window are used as a place for drying clothes. In total, there are sixteen households in the two houses. In addition to the front building of the living room that their family uses for themselves, they can earn a total of one hundred thirty to forty yuan in rent each month. The rent, house tax, and electricity bills that their family pays add up to less than ninety yuan, so they can sit back and earn forty to fifty yuan each month.

In addition to the husband and wife, there are two children and a maid, totaling five people; since there are few people, one front building is enough for living. Among the fifteen tenant households in these two houses, men and women are mixed, and of course many people have free time and want to find some entertainment and leisure methods, so the Sun family's radio has a very strong influence, attracting co-residents to come into the room to listen up close. Sister Sun is also very friendly, inviting everyone to play a game of mahjong, diligently providing cigarettes and leisure fruits, and only taking a small amount of head money in the game that does not hurt integrity, which is also very popular among the co-residents. Mr. Sun also has many friends, (which shows his hospitality and has the flavor of Lord Mengchang) often using playing cards to connect feelings, or containing other side effects, besides those who are specifically focused on gambling and losing money.

Although Mr. Sun has no occupation, he has a talent for socializing, and everyone who meets him once is attracted as a confidant. His ability to develop outwards, if used in business, should be able to get very satisfactory results! But he does not do business, so his body is not subject to any restrictions, and he is much more leisurely and comfortable than ordinary people, even up to the chairman of the National Government! When he encounters the side of the old calendar festival, he books a day show in a theater, borrows some nice name, and distributes and sells tickets separately; fortunately, he has many friends, and the sales of tickets always have considerable results. Every time he holds this trick called "da chou feng" (draw windfall) by the Shanghai people, he can earn as little as three or four hundred and as much as seven or eight hundred yuan.

Mr. Sun's filial piety is also praised by his friends. Every year, he always holds memorial ceremonies for his deceased parents, and sometimes even for his ancestors, on the anniversary of their death. He sends out invitations to invite people to eat a meal, how can people be embarrassed not to send a little gift? Thus, as a result of commemorating the ancestors, Mr. Sun's pocket can be filled with several hundred yuan again.

These few fixed incomes, within a year, already amount to four or five thousand yuan, his family's expenses naturally do not need to rely on the income of permanent employment, can be very sufficient, and the situation is also very generous. This Mr. Sun does not bother to emulate the "calculating" of those loafers (that deserves people's hatred), and takes this route to make money, in terms of personality, he is indeed much better than them.

Education News

Middle and Primary School Health Education Design Committee 209

Yesterday's First Meeting

Passed Eight Important Cases

(Nanjing, 27th Dispatch) The Middle and Primary School Health Education Design Committee held its first meeting on the 26th. Chairman Gu Shusen resolved: (1) To appoint Jin Saishan, Zhu Zhanggeng, Zhang Chongde, Wu Yan'yin, and Dai Yingguan to draft standards for middle and primary school health expenses and the allocation of their uses, to be completed within January of next year. To request the Ministry of Education to order the education departments and bureaus of all provinces and cities to include school health expenses in the local education expense budget starting from the 24th academic year. (2) To approve the school health implementation plan compiled by the Health Experiment Office. To request the Ministry of Education to issue a circular to the education departments and bureaus of all provinces and cities, instructing all schools to adopt it. Also, to designate Zhu Zhanggeng and Zhang Chongde (middle school), and Zhang Wei (rural primary school) to be responsible for the implementation plans for middle schools and rural primary schools. After the plans are drafted, to request the Ministry of Education to designate several schools for pilot testing, and to promulgate them after revision. (3) To designate educational personnel in middle and primary schools to be responsible for managing the school's health, and to assist school health technical personnel in promoting school health matters. Regarding the proposal to request the Ministry of Education to issue a circular to the education departments and bureaus of all provinces and cities, and the competent educational authorities, to establish health education committees in conjunction with local health authorities to improve health education and school health in middle and primary schools, it was resolved to request the Ministry of Education to issue a circular to the education departments and bureaus of all provinces and cities, and the competent educational authorities, and to instruct middle and primary schools to designate personnel (one director of teaching or director of discipline for middle schools, and one grade teacher for primary schools) to be specifically responsible for managing the school's health, and to assist school health technical personnel in promoting school health matters. (4) To organize a specialized committee to design standards for middle and primary school building construction, classroom desks and chairs, and health equipment. It was resolved: 1. Regarding health equipment standards, to request the Ministry of Health to draft them. Regarding physiological health teaching equipment, to request the Health Education Department of National Central University to draft them. Regarding the healthcare part, to request the Ministry of Health to draft them. 3. Regarding classroom desks and chairs, to request the Health Education Committee of Beijing to conduct a concrete study. 4. Regarding school building construction, to request the Health Education Committee of Shanghai to conduct a study, and to request Zhang Wei to preside over it. (5) To request the confirmation and promulgation of the (School Health Lecture Series) measures. It was resolved: 1. The Ministry of Education will entrust the central health authorities to run school health lecture series. If education departments and bureaus of all provinces and cities need such talents, they should immediately send personnel to participate. 2. To request the Ministry of Education to issue a circular to the education departments and bureaus of all provinces and cities to add a school health course when holding summer lecture series. 3. To request the provinces and cities that have already established health education committees to hold school health summer lecture series, and to convene school health personnel in charge to attend the lectures. Subsequently, a temporary proposal was made: (6) To request the Ministry of Education to pay attention to cultivating health education teachers. It was resolved to request the Ministry of Education to order the education colleges of all universities and all normal schools to pay attention to cultivating health education teachers for middle and primary schools. (7) To request the central government to allocate funds to subsidize research on health education issues. It was resolved to appoint Zhu Zhanggeng and Zhang Chongde to draft an outline for the research on (standards for student physical development), and to request the China Foundation for the Promotion of Education and Culture to allocate funds for subsidies. (8) To request the Ministry of Education to issue a circular to the education departments and bureaus of all provinces and cities to pay attention to school health inspections. It was resolved to request Zhu Zhanggeng to draft health inspection standards and submit them to the Ministry of Education for reference.

Vocational School Graduates' Admission to Higher Education Not Restricted by Entrance Examination 213

The Ministry of Education has already implemented the entrance examination system for middle schools and normal schools. After announcing the entrance examination subjects for physical education normal schools, it will also be implemented in the future. However, because there are many types of vocational schools and the curriculum standards are difficult to unify, the Ministry of Education has compiled outlines of teaching materials and other documents, ordering the schools to hold entrance examinations. For the time being, there are no regulations. Previously, the Shanxi Education Department inquired about the admission methods for vocational schools. The Ministry of Education recently replied that the current admission to higher education for vocational schools is not restricted by the entrance examination.

Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau Reissues Registration Certificates for Cultural Organizations 225

▲ Each Organization Must Go to the Education Bureau to Collect Them

In recent years, the addresses of many registered cultural organizations have been unclear. Some have not reported due to relocation, and some have been dissolved invisibly due to the Shanghai war. Now, for the purpose of reorganization, the Municipal Education Bureau has specially reprinted registration certificates for distribution. From now until the end of January of the 24th year, all registered cultural organizations must go to the bureau to exchange for certificates. If they fail to exchange within the deadline, the registration will be revoked.

Zhou Houchu Arrives in Shanghai to Convene the Committee to Reduce the Workload of Middle School Students 226

▲ This Afternoon at 4 PM

In order to improve secondary education, the Jiangsu Education Department organized a committee to study various training issues. Since the implementation of the entrance examination system, the most important issue in secondary education is the heavy workload and intellectual burden that middle school students universally feel. They are busy all day long and do not have enough time. As a result, young people neglect their physical and mental cultivation, extracurricular activities, and independent research, which greatly affects educational efficiency and youth training. Director Zhou of the Education Department recognized this and organized a committee to study the issue of reducing student workload. He appointed Zhou Houchu, Principal of Provincial Yangzhou Middle School, Zheng Tonghe, Principal of Shanghai Middle School, Cao Chu, Principal of Zhenjiang Normal School, Zhang Haicheng, Principal of Nanjing Middle School, Tang Zhicai, Principal of Suzhou Agricultural School, and Peng Weiji, Principal of Changzhou Middle School, as seven committee members, and designated Zhou Houchu as the convener. After Zhou was appointed, he wrote to each committee member to ask them to convene teachers from each department at their respective schools to conduct preliminary research and scheduled a formal meeting in Shanghai this afternoon (28th) at 4 PM. Zhou has already arrived in Shanghai and said that this research will seek effective methods that are easy to implement and do not hinder the scope of departmental regulations. The department also instructed that the issue of tutor time and work allocation should be discussed together.

Peiming Girls' Middle School on McLean Road has always been known for its entertainment performances. Minli Girls' Middle School to Hold New School Building Completion Ceremony on New Year's Day 230

Flag Raising at 8:00 AM, Scout Inspection at 10:00 AM

Completion Ceremony at 2:00 PM, Entertainment Gala at 6:00 PM

Minli Girls' Middle School on Wenmiao Road in the South City was established 30 years ago and is a major female school in this port. Since the reorganization last semester, it has become more vigorous. Headmaster Tong Xingbai believes that the original school buildings are not sufficient to accommodate the increasing number of students. In order to ensure that newcomers are not turned away, she especially obtained the consent of the school board to build a five-story flat-roofed building of reinforced concrete on the original site as a new school building. It has now been completed in stages. A flag-raising ceremony will be held at 8:00 AM on New Year's Day, a scout inspection will be held at 10:00 AM, a completion ceremony for the new school building will be held at 2:00 PM, and an entertainment gala will begin at 6:00 PM. There are many programs and it is quite exciting. It has also been decided to exhibit achievements on that day, and all departments are collecting them, so the work is quite busy.

Huadong Girls' Middle School Adds Spring Junior High School Class 231

Huadong Girls' Middle School in this city has perfect management and remarkable achievements. The school recognizes that most secondary schools for girls in this city do not have spring start-up classes. Therefore, the primary school graduates in the spring have no way to go to school every month. Therefore, starting from the second semester of the 23rd year, that is, the spring of the 24th year, a new freshman class for the first grade of junior high school will be added in the spring to increase the opportunity for girls to go to school. The school's junior high school grades one, two, and three in the autumn, senior high school general subjects grades one, two, and three, and business subjects grades one and two all accept transfer students, and the entrance examination is scheduled for January 22nd.

The repertoire includes Golden Stage Sitting in the Palace, Pearl Curtain Village Starting the Escort, Catching and Releasing the Lodging House, etc. All of them are carefully crafted. The ticket price is two jiao, and it is thought that the streets will be very lively at that time.

Special Article

German Middle School Teacher Training (3) Zhu Zhenxun 234

2. Teacher Examination: Teacher examinations involve practical training, which usually lasts more than two years. The first year of training is limited to local education research groups. The main training items during this year include general individual observation and research, as well as participation in all educational activities in the school. In addition, there are speeches, application of foreign language conversation, handicrafts, natural science experiments, physical education, and journalism training. The second year of training is within the district education group. This year's training items include detailed understanding of the theory of each subject and systematic acquisition of teaching experience. In addition, attention must be paid to independent work and obedience to the guidance of consultants. The internship teaching time is stipulated to be eight hours per week. Internship teaching is not allowed in two schools at the same time. During internship teaching, special emphasis should be placed on independent and continuous work. The nature of this work is particularly noteworthy in the teacher examination committee.

Teacher examinations are conducted by a special examination committee. This special committee is composed of the chairman and vice-chairman, middle school teacher inspectors, and three well-known middle school instructors. There is at least one female member in this committee to handle the registration and examination procedures for female candidates. Whether the applicant is allowed to take the exam is determined by the chairman based on the certificate of the instructor in the middle school designated by the applicant for internship, the report of the applicant's consultant, and the criticism of the middle school inspector.

The method of teacher examination is the same as the degree examination, divided into written and oral examinations. The written examination is only one paper, and the topic is selected within the scope specified by the applicant's consultant. The oral examination includes demonstration teaching methods and educational inquiries.

Anyone can participate in the teacher examination. Those who fail the examination may be allowed to retake the exam with the permission of the special examination committee. The date is determined by the committee. The examination fee for the teacher examination is 40 marks. Those who pass the teacher examination can obtain a middle school teacher's certificate and be included in the register of candidates for permanent middle school teacher positions. Under the legal protection of national preparatory officials, they have the right to receive salaries. The annual salary for those who have been hired as middle school teachers is 3,000 to 4,000 marks. Other candidate middle school teachers who are on the register but have not been hired can also enjoy the national salary, but the amount is only 80% of the salary of a formal middle school teacher. Middle school teacher positions are appointed in turn according to the candidate register, except in special circumstances. In short, candidate middle school teachers must wait a long time to obtain a permanent middle school teacher position.

Although it is extremely difficult to obtain a German middle school teacher position, the number of men and women who eagerly seek this position is still large. Therefore, the special examination committee often raises the standards of examination and selection to limit the number of people. In Germany, where the population is surplus and lacks colonies, middle school teacher positions with permanent guarantees are often noticed by general university and vocational school students. According to the Prussian Ministry of Education's Popular Education Monthly published on August 20, 1930, the number of German university students preparing to take the national middle school teacher examination in 1929-1930 was 2,400 to 1,934. That is, this year, the number of candidates on the middle school teacher register has increased to 7,000 to 8,000, but only 1,600 can obtain permanent middle school teacher positions. This shows the strictness of Germany's selection of middle school teachers, which is unmatched by any country in the world. (The End)

Free Talk

Melancholy Literature 235

— Qi

Saltikov-Shchedrin (saltikovshch)ekrin) said in a sketch called "One Day in My County":

"What to write? What heroic achievements to sing? There are no heroic achievements｜That place only has melancholy ordinariness, no heroes｜Their place is occupied by those who tremble in fear｜What should I do? Clearly, I can only grieve with you, and be a chronicler of sighs... But how difficult this is! ... The world is miserable, and I grieve with it, the world sighs｜I also sigh with it, and I also ask readers to grieve with me."

These few words reveal the greatest characteristic of old Russian literature. Under the gloomy conditions of Tsarist rule, the description of the wounds of Russian life became the main content of literary works. Whether it is Gogol's and Chekhov's satire and humor, or Turgenev's lyrical tone and Dostoevsky's meticulous psychological anatomy, they all carry a dark and melancholy shadow and a heavy feeling of sadness.

George Brandes said in an article commenting on Turgenev: "Turgenev's melancholy is essentially the melancholy of the Slavic race with its defects and tragic aspects, and is a legitimate descendant of Slavic folk songs. ... Gogol's melancholy comes from despair. When Dostoevsky expresses the same melancholy, it is because his heart sympathizes with those who have been trampled on and great sinners. Tolstoy's melancholy is based on his religious fate theory."

When we read these writers' works, we are often infected by their melancholy atmosphere. This melancholy is not the pleasant sentimentality of "cherishing spring and grieving autumn", but a kind of heavy mood of being overwhelmed by the surrounding chaos and darkness. The author sometimes treats you with a smile, but that kind of smile is not light, but a tragic smile. The so-called tearsthrdnghlaugbter is the characteristic of Gogol's and Chekhov's art.

In "How Ivan Ivanovich and Ivan Nikiforovich Quarrelled," Gogol did his best to ridicule the ugliness of landlords and bureaucrats, making you unable to help but laugh no matter what. This story starts completely as a merry farce, but at the end it is also shrouded in an air of melancholy, and ends with the following characteristic sentence: "This world is very gloomy, gentlemen." Belinsky (belinsdy) said that Gogol's works "always reveal sad and depressed feelings", which is not an exaggeration.

Chekhov's melancholy also once swept the Russian literary world. I don't know how many readers were infected with "Chekhov-style emotions". The disappointment and pessimism of the protagonist in his "Gloomy Story" towards himself, towards the gray reality of life, and towards those mediocre and humble people around him, is a reflection of "Chekhov-style emotions". His plays, such as the famous "The Cherry Orchard" and "Uncle Vanya", are all filled with gloomy, decadent, and negative emotions.

Although Russian writers were suffocated by the darkness and ugliness of the surrounding world, and melancholy spasms arose on their faces, the yearning and pursuit for a bright future, like an unquenchable fire, always burned in their hearts. This is the greatest part of Russian literature. Even in Chekhov's gloomy works, one can see the longing for the dawn of a brilliant future life. Vershinin in "Three Sisters" said the following: "In two or three hundred years, human life will probably become dazzlingly beautiful and brilliant."

But in less than twenty or thirty years, more than ten times faster than Chekhov expected, the "beautiful and brilliant" life that Chekhov dreamed of has been realized on earth. What is reflected in today's Russian literature is naturally no longer "melancholy ordinariness", but truly "heroes" and "great achievements".

Kunming (Part 1) 236

— Li Qiao

｜Local Impression Notes｜

People who have never been to Yunnan always feel a little scared when they mention Yunnan: as if the place is very far away, barbaric, and has poisonous miasma. No one has ever dared to go, and if you go, you will die! Therefore, even the old men of Xinfeng who were conscripted into the army, upon hearing that the team was going to Yunnan, would rather pick up a stone and break their arms than follow the team to their deaths!

This kind of fear and prejudice against Yunnan has always been very serious. In fact, why is Yunnan like what they imagine? ｜

Yunnan has its own special flavor. In this vast realm of towering mountains and primitive nature, although some appear wild and rugged, there are many places of "green mountains and clear waters" that you cannot imagine.

For example, Kunming? What kind of place do you think it is?

It is a beauty hiding in the deep mountains, not yet discovered by people. Although the dress is a bit outdated, it is enough to intoxicate you.

When a traveler, carrying such a tired body, is brought to Kunming alone by the Yunnan-Vietnam train, it will give you sweet tenderness, as if it were your long-lost mistress. According to your likes, it will satisfy you in every way.

If you are a worshiper of cities, when you arrive in Kunming, you will not feel that it does not have any urban atmosphere! In 遒裏 there are neat Western-style shops, wide and flat roads, cars, rickshaws, bicycles, constantly coming and going; people rushing to join the excitement, walking so crowded on both sides of the street. The shops on both sides of the road display dazzling goods, and the clear sound of the gramophone is constantly broadcast from the shops with cheap signs, which seems so strangely lively.

From day to night, the place that is always crowded with people is the playground without sorrow. There is a sound movie theater and a silent movie theater, and the theater also has a Peking opera singer and a Yunnan opera singer. In addition, there are many small tea gardens where you can listen to the board-banging opera, where you can just make a pot of tea and sit and listen.

Luxurious taverns and elegant coffee shops are also available in this place. Unfortunately, there are no female attendants, otherwise, it would be enough for the general playboys to be happy.

Kunming also has a road like Shanghai's Avenue Joffre. This quiet place is full of foreign residences and hotels, located next to the Panlong River. In the evening, you can walk slowly on the river bank, look at the slowly flowing river water, and the electric lights in the opposite room with their attractive magic power shining brightly on the water, which is really interesting!

If you think this is too monotonous and does not fit your ideal of loving scenery, then you might as well go to Cuihu Lake for a walk? That place is located on the northwest side of Kunming City. Wuhua Mountain, Yuantong Mountain, and Gongyuan Slope stand out around it. A clear small river surrounds the lake, and there are two long embankments full of green willows in the lake. Because these two embankments intersect each other, the entire lake is divided into four parts. At the intersection point, there is the famous Haixin Pavilion. No matter what day it is, you can see many men and women leaning on the railings, leisurely throwing fried rice candy, and admiring the fish swimming in the pool.

If you have been in Kunming for a long time and feel that strolling the streets during the day is a bit tasteless, then you might as well go out at night. Kunming at night has some special flavors. It is best to go to the antique stalls on Wenming Street: it is very lively there at night. All kinds of things are sold there. Anything you can't buy on the street during the day can be bought there at night. However, please pay attention: there are often many "slickers" holding something and pretending to sell it to the antique dealers. The antique dealers also deliberately give him (or her) a high price, but the seller is still a bit unwilling, and the two sides are struggling there. At this time, if you do not understand the trick, and think that the antique dealers are willing to give him (or her) such a price, then the thing must be very valuable, and you rashly add a few more cents, then you will definitely be fooled.

Kunming people have so many treacherous skills, but this is where they suffer a great loss. They only care about the present and not the future. They think that as long as they can deceive others, that's enough.

Due to the influence of the living environment, the nature of Kunming people is mostly very weak. Needless to say, women, many men do not even dare to go out, and just die guarding their homes all their lives. They love vanity, love to put on a show, and no matter who it is, women must be called "Madam", and men must be called "Master". They don't care whether they have food to eat or not, but face is something that cannot be neglected. Even when they reach the point where they rely on their daughters selling prostitution to make a living, their facade is still dressed up very beautifully.

Returning from the Volcano (7) 237

— Lan Ru

After they left, I still stayed alone at the edge of the crater, mourning those young men from foreign countries whose names are unknown, those brave warriors who sacrificed for love!

The smoke coming out of the crater, at first, rose up like the black smoke spewed out by a train engine when it first starts ... puff ... puff ... Then, slowly rising dense black smoke turned into wisps of gray clouds. Finally, the gray clouds slowly faded away.

The circumference of the crater is more than 30 feet, but no one knows the depth. Last year, the volcanic expedition organized by the Yomiuri Shimbun only reached halfway, because there was no air, and the volcano was about to explode, so they could not move forward. They had seen many young men and women who were crushed to pieces. Although I could not see that tragic death, looking at the crater with blood stains, I knew that it had devoured many promising young men and women.

Perhaps everyone has what is called conscience? Even a person whose rationality is like iron, usually opposes love suicide and opposes suicide! Cursing them as weak, worthless! But once you come to the volcano, everyone will turn curses into pity, and dislike into love. Everyone has such a thought: "People who come here to commit suicide are really brave and great."

Originally, people who commit suicide do so because there is no way out of life, or they feel tired of life. After being heartbroken or unemployed, they can no longer endure the pain, so they make up their minds to end their lives in a very short time and gain permanent relief. But people who come to the volcano to commit suicide are different! They must go through the crowded life of a night of sailing, go through more than forty miles of mountain paths, the labor of trekking, traverse the vast desert, and traverse the steep and terrible lava, and then offer their lives to the volcano as a sacrifice, flesh and blood flying everywhere, and their bodies are incomplete. Why don't they take poison or jump into the sea? It's a bit too silly to suffer so much hardship and pain before death, isn't it?

The guards at the crater told us: "Most people who jump into the volcano do so in the evening at dusk, and it is rare in the morning." He also said: "I haven't seen anyone jump into the volcano today." This means that someone had jumped down a few days ago.

At the highest point of the crater, there is a round reflector, from which you can see the infinitely deep mountain and the monument to the Yomiuri Shimbun's exploration, which is also near this mirror.

New Star 238

— Prism

We often see the term "new star," in writings about newly popular actors, in movie advertisements, and on radio programs. However, these are merely rhetorical metaphors; we rarely hear about true new stars. In the heavens, perhaps a new star is discovered only once every few decades. Nature is always so dull and unchanging, unlike man-made "new stars," which can be created at will. Naturally, these celestial new stars cannot be as frequently in the public eye as their human counterparts; but precisely because they are so rare, they should be far more precious than the overused term "new star."

The term "new star" is also called "temporary star," and in Chinese, it's known as "guest star." Among these three names, "temporary star" seems the most appropriate. "Guest star" implies that the star comes from one place and goes to another, which is not in accordance with the facts. "New star" suggests a sudden birth and a permanent addition to the sky, but in reality, all new stars exist long before they are discovered, and they eventually fade away. A new star cannot shine forever, so using "new star" to describe a person actually carries a somewhat ominous connotation. "Temporary star" describes a sudden brightening, from being invisible to the naked eye to becoming visible, and then disappearing again. It appears temporary to us, but as for the star's existence, we cannot easily trace its origins. Therefore, even this is not a scientific term. In modern astronomy, according to Pickering's classification, it belongs to the first class of variable stars.

The importance of variable stars in modern astronomy is almost unparalleled. Cepheid variable stars are used to determine the distance of fixed star clusters and nebulae; eclipsing binary stars can determine the orbits of binary stars; and long-period variable stars indicate how stars evolve. New stars are particularly good sources of reference. Mira, a variable star, is most helpful in understanding new stars. At its brightest, it is a fairly bright second-magnitude star; at its dimmest, it reaches tenth magnitude. Our naked eye can barely see stars of the sixth magnitude, so this star appears and disappears to us. However, it recurs approximately every 330 days, so we can be confident that it will not disappear completely.

New stars are a more extreme example. At their brightest, they can reach the luminosity of Venus; at their dimmest, they may reach the twenty-first magnitude (the limit of what telescopes can see) or even complete darkness. Whether they have a cycle, humans with their short lifespan and history cannot yet answer. However, some old new stars have disappeared and are now seen as faint stars in their original positions. Astronomers probably visit them from time to time, and perhaps one day they will find them brightening again, resolving a question for us.

The common explanation is that the sudden brightening of a new star is due to external forces causing it to explode (as the Reuters report on the new star on the 25th said). The fate after the explosion is death. This can also lead to our reveries. After it becomes lightless and powerless, it may be drawn in by the force that caused it to explode and gradually become a planet, and eventually, life may arise on it. We will never know all this, as the time scale is too long.

The telegraph report states that the newly discovered star is 1,500 light-years away and that its brightening occurred around the time of the fall of the Roman Empire. This already indicates a vast amount of time, but even after another 1,500 years, it will not have died out. The figure of 1,500 light-years seems questionable, as it seems impossible to determine the distance of a single star to be more than a thousand light-years.

According to the report, this new star is located in the Hercules constellation, which is probably what is now translated as the Hercules constellation. At our latitude, this constellation sinks below the northwest horizon by 6 PM in December and rises from the northeast at 6 AM. If it weren't for the continuous cloudy weather these days, we might have had a chance to see it. Otherwise, the Hercules constellation originally has no bright stars, and the sudden appearance of a bright star would be noticeable to anyone familiar with the stars. Wasn't it discovered by an amateur astronomer in England? Why didn't the observatory discover it first? That's because astronomers mainly use telescopes to search the distant sky, only seeing a very small corner of it, so they have fewer opportunities to pay attention to the entire sky than amateurs. If there were a telescopic new star in the sky today and we didn't know where it was, we might search for it with a telescope for years without finding it.

Flies (1) 239

— By Pianndlle, Translated by Xi Dichen

As soon as they reached the bottom of the village, they walked extra fast, gasping for breath - Crawl, crawl up here! - They crawled up the chalky, rugged shore - now they even used their hands - grabbing tightly as they climbed - because the hobnailed boots they were wearing - oh God! - were slippery.

Their faces flushed crimson, they crawled to the shore, and the women gathered noisily around the village spring turned their heads to look. Weren't those the two Totolisi brothers? Yes, it was them - Salo and Nelli. Ah, poor souls! Why were they running like that! The brother Nelli, because he was already exhausted, stopped for a moment, wanting to catch his breath and answer the women, but Salo pulled him away.

"Our cousin Cheru!" Nelli then turned his head and said: He raised his hand, seemingly to give three blessings. The women let out cries of sympathy and terror. One of them asked loudly:

"Who is it?"

"Nameless: God!" Nelli shouted from afar.

The brothers crossed the small square and headed towards the doctor's house.

× × × × × × × × ×

Dr. Xituoluo, wearing a shirt, his face unshaven for at least ten days, his eyes swollen, shuffled around the room in a pair of old slippers, holding a pitiful-looking sick child in his arms, with a sallow complexion and skin and bones, about nine years old.

His wife had been in bed for eleven months; besides the eldest child he was holding, there were six other children in the house, all dressed in rags, dirty and boisterous; the whole house was upside down, in chaos - it was a ruin; leftover food, fruit peels, and garbage were all piled on the floor; the chairs and stools were broken, the armchairs had no cushions, and the beds hadn't been made in who knows how long, the sheets torn into strips, because the children often had pillow fights on the beds for fun - these poor things!

Only in the room that had once been the reception room, a large photograph hanging on the wall remained intact; it was a photo of the doctor himself, taken in his youth, when he had just obtained his degree: dressed neatly, radiating a smile.

Authorities Firmly Deny Rumors of Post-Holiday Gold Market Crash 241

Hopes Shattered, Dreams Dissipated 242

Breaking the Seventy Yuan Barrier 243

Plunging Twelve Yuan at a Time 244

Due to the bank holiday suspension of trading for two days, the gold market fell upon reopening yesterday. Reports indicate that Chairman Chiang himself has strongly denied the rumors, shattering hopes for favorable news. The Chinese Commercial Bank vigorously offered drafts, leading to a generally weak market sentiment throughout the day. In the morning, overseas silver markets during the holiday period and the silver price in the Montevideo forward market rose slightly, but exchange rates shrank slightly, spot gold in London fell by half a penny, the Central Bank's official exchange rate for both British and American currencies remained unchanged, the customs gold unit shrank slightly by one li, the standard price for gold bars was 1,012.9 yuan, and the silver equalization tax remained unchanged. As a result, off-market trading opened, initially quoted at 81.2 yuan. However, due to reports that Chairman Chiang firmly denied any inflationary policies, public confidence was greatly restored, dispelling rumors unfavorable to sellers. The trend toward selling became a torrent, immediately breaking the 80 yuan barrier. Large holders wanted to dump their holdings, but lacked counterparties, causing the decline to be quite severe, gradually falling to 71.2 yuan, before slightly stabilizing. The Central Bank's official exchange rate was announced, and all holders became more cautious. Large holders took the opportunity to buy at the low, causing a rebound. However, the opening in the morning was still low, and although public confidence had not yet stabilized, the selling trend continued. However, because the exchange market was loose but normal, and banks still had an appetite, activity in the buying market caused a rebound. Shortly thereafter, it was learned that the HSBC's official exchange rate was announced, with the pound rising 0.125 and the dollar rising 0.25, causing public apprehension and another downturn. However, because the Central Bank and HSBC were still purchasing foreign exchange, the market stabilized after the decline. Shortly thereafter, the silver equalization tax was announced, reduced by 0.25, with only 5.5% being collected. With the pound exchange rate calculated at 1 shilling 5 pence 0.375, the upward trend was hindered. Chinese Banks Vigorously Offer Drafts, Foreign Exchange Trends Loosen 245

Yesterday's foreign exchange market was stimulated by overseas telegrams that trading had been compressed for two days. London large bills were up 0.0625 for both near and far terms, U.S. dollars were up 0.125, the Montevideo forward silver price was up one li, London spot gold was down half a penny, the pound against the dollar was down 0.375, the dollar against the pound was down 0.375, the pound against the franc was unchanged, and the dollar against the franc was up 0.375. Supplement to the Shanghai Shen Bao

Random Thoughts

British Emperor Hosts Feast for the Poor 283

— Chao Jiao

It is reported that the British Emperor hosted a feast for 700 poor people in the Whitechapel on Christmas Day. It is said that this is a regular annual custom. The Emperor hosting a feast for the poor - what a delightful piece of news this is! The Emperor is recognized as the most supreme and noble figure in British society, and the so-called 700 poor people, although not all are so impoverished as to have nowhere to set foot (I imagine that if they were truly so impoverished as to have nowhere to set foot, they would not in reality be so honored as to be invited to a feast by the Emperor; the poor who are invited to the Emperor's feast, although called poor, must still have some, albeit not large, but somewhat small, history of some kind. Otherwise, why would the poor who are invited to the feast be limited to just these 700?), but they are generally some extremely destitute so-called poor people. These 700 poor people who have always been extremely destitute, suddenly sit together with the one who has always been called the most supreme and noble Emperor, toasting face to face (but whether they are actually toasting face to face is still a question; perhaps the Emperor sends a representative to host these poorly-dressed poor people - that may very well be the case), shaking hands and exchanging pleasantries (?), just imagine, what an honorable thing this must be.

However, we find it very regrettable that the so-called poor people whom the Emperor deigns to show favor to in this instance (as happens every year) are unfortunately limited to 700, and that the feast is limited to only one occasion. How can the many other poor people (Britain has three million unemployed people) all be able to be graciously invited to this feast, and, even for those poor people who are able to be invited to this feast, how can they all be able to eat that extremely rich meal gifted by the Emperor every year, every day? This then becomes an extremely serious and difficult-to-solve problem.

The Emperor can prepare some not very rich (as I imagine, probably not very rich at all) wine and dishes every Christmas to invite a small portion of the poor to a feast, but he cannot distribute more bread so that a wider population of the unemployed can all have something to eat. This is a very regrettable event. How will the Emperor use what method to ensure that the general poor can just eat coarse black bread and be satisfied? This is a highly debatable question.

Rickshaw Puller Zhang Fusheng 284

— Bai Yang

I already knew that rickshaws were in use in my hometown; however, besides the main road that can barely accommodate rubber wheels, the other small roads are so bumpy that even when sitting in a sedan chair, one feels like they're about to fall apart. So, I thought that rickshaws were only used by a few local gentry youths to show off on the main street. But, when I stepped off the train carrying my luggage, I was surrounded by a swarm of rickshaw pullers. Looking ahead, I saw nearly a hundred rickshaws lined up along both sides of the road. This was beyond my expectations. Seeing such a display, it was undeniable that the small roads where outsiders stumbled three times for every step must have been improved. Otherwise, the rickshaw company's losses on the vehicles would be too great, and where would the business for nearly a hundred rickshaws come from?

As I stood there dumbfounded, suddenly a huge

Page 18

hand snatched my luggage. At the same time, a shout of "Young Master" came from who knows which rickshaw puller.

Helplessly, my gaze followed the giant arm upward. It turned out to be a short, farmer-like man. Looking at his face, where his nose and eyebrows were almost connected, I clearly remembered that he was my classmate Zhang Fusheng from elementary school. At this moment, seeing that the business had already been taken, the group of rickshaw pullers swarmed towards the next arrival.

Zhang Fusheng took my luggage and said in a commanding tone:

"This way, Young Master!"

He darted out of the station's wooden fence like a monkey, placed my luggage on the footpad of a rickshaw, and squatted between the two shafts, waiting for me to get in.

When I sat in his rickshaw, he lifted the shafts and whistled, as if to show off to his companions, and then took off running.

The small road extending in front of the station was originally lined with fields. Farmers, for the convenience of drawing water, had dug large gaps along the road. Moreover, the roots of several large trees along the road stretched into the middle of the road like mountain ranges. If one walked at night, a careless step could send you tumbling into the rice paddies, covered in mud. Now, these giant old trees had been cut down, and the gaps had been filled in. Naturally, the tree roots that obstructed pedestrians were also gone. So, although it wasn't as good as Shanghai's Bubbling Well Road, there was no danger of crashing into the rice paddies with the rickshaw.

Fusheng pulled the rickshaw especially fast. He had already taken the lead. As the road ahead gradually narrowed, I couldn't help but blurt out:

"Fusheng, pull it slowly."

Fusheng was naturally surprised that an outsider could call out his name. He quickly stopped the rickshaw, turned around, and asked:

"Young Master is a local?"

"Don't you recognize me? We studied at ×× Elementary School together."

Then he slowed down, turned around several times to examine me, and finally said:

"It's been too many years. I can't remember what Young Master's name is!"

"That's right, you were a year above me. I heard that you were sent from the school to higher elementary school?" I chatted with him in detail.

"Oh, I remember," he said. "Young Master is called Zhu ××, right? The principal sent me to higher elementary school, but only the first year was free. The second year, my family couldn't afford the fees, so my dad didn't want me to study anymore. At that time, my family had a few acres of land to farm ourselves. We originally had to hire people to help with the farming, but I helped out as half a worker. But in recent years, it's really been unlucky..."

The rickshaw had reached a fork in the road. He turned west and asked me again:

I replied, "Yes." He continued, saying:

"In recent years, the land hasn't yielded enough. I sold a few acres of land and now I'm farming for others. Now that the new rice is on the market, I come out to pull a rickshaw in my spare time to earn some money. Did Young Master make a fortune in Shanghai?"

He seemed to be waiting for my answer, and stopped talking. But I didn't answer him, even though he turned around twice to look at my face.

When we arrived home, I paid the fare. I felt a sorrow like being oppressed by a thick fog in my heart.

Zhao Family Village Shrouded in the Early Winter Dusk 285

— Bu Yang

It was an early winter dusk

The sky was like the face of a fallen person, kissing the distant treetops with its ashen gray.

The wind vigorously carried the unmanaged fallen leaves across the fields after the autumn harvest.

The stone road leading to the town was turning fish-belly white in the vastness. At the corner of the road stood a tall banner, more than ten feet high, with the words "Zhao Family Village Regular Force" written on it. It was erected after conscription. It roared proudly in the wind, as if it had the mission of protecting the village's security.

Zhao Family Village, surrounded by dozens of bungalows and multi-story buildings, judging from its appearance, it must have seen the enthronement of the Tongzhi Emperor. At this time, smoke was rising from the chimneys of every house, like signal fires. Several village women with blue cloths covering their heads were straining their throats, calling out the names of their husbands and sons at the corner of the road. Then, farmers in blue cloth jackets and snot-nosed cowherds, as if summoned, shuffled with hunched backs from the small bridge into the white-board doors facing the river.

Several peddlers returning from the market in the town three miles away moved like scales on the fish-belly white road. They were worried that their mothers and wives were waiting for them to eat dinner, but looking at the many unsold oranges, bananas, candies, and cakes remaining on their shoulders, they feared they couldn't make the accounting. So, they shouted with a hundredfold advertising power in front of every eave, and the seductive sound waves stirred up a group of children who had just returned from school. They all used their black, shiny eyes to pick out which load was good, which one was big, which one wasn't rotten. After several business disputes, they satisfied both parties' desires with a cheaper price.

The children scattered, and feeling that their pockets were much heavier, their steps suddenly became lighter, and they went to another small road, again like scales.

The throats of people on boats echoed in the reeds. The fisherman who had just risen from the water, wearing a light cotton coat, was sitting on the bow of the boat, sipping from a wine bottle. The fisherwoman with a bun was busy in the cabin, sorting out the day's harvest. Several people who had gone out to make money with great difficulty were bowing and haggling over the price of fish and crabs with them at the dock. Only when they felt it was cheap in their mental calculations did they take out one or two double-cent coins from their close-fitting pockets and drop a string of crab with white foam and river fish wagging their tails into the boat.

The sharp sound of the Ningguan Road last bus's horn echoed through the evening air, followed by a series of sparse dog barks.

Several travelers carrying luggage returned from the station two miles away. They all knocked on their own doors with a joyful heart, and they all prepared a set of unexpected emotions to give to their beloveds.

The pen of Father Time added a night scene more realistic than the painter, and the surroundings were quiet. Darkness swallowed everything in Zhao Family Village.

Sketch of a Decadent Village "Mom, I want to eat too!" 286

Stalin in Swaddling Clothes 287

— Qujiang

The majestic Caucasus Mountains dominate the crucial route between Europe and Asia. It is a meeting point of all places, where over a hundred ethnic groups live, and tribalism and imperialism run parallel. This is the birthplace of Bolshevik leader Stalin.

In the village of Gori in Georgia, there was a family named Diugashvili, whose ancestors were farmers and cobblers. When farming could no longer sustain them, Vissarion from the Djnagashvili family left his hometown and drifted to the neighboring village of Ogri, working as a worker in a shoe factory.

Vissarion's wife, named Ekaterina, was a Georgian woman. Georgian women marry at the age of thirteen or fourteen because they mature earlier than ordinary women. By the age of thirty-five, they are already old. Therefore, Ekaterina became a mother very early and continued to have three children, but they all died soon after. The fourth child was about to be born around Christmas. She was a devout Christian woman, and she prayed to God to give her a son who would grow up. She named the child Joseph in advance.

Joseph Stalin was born on December 21, 1879. Ekaterina was only twenty years old at the time. She nicknamed Stalin "Soso." "Soso" was originally the name of a beloved animal in Georgia. Ekaterina had great plans for the child and held ardent ambitions. She even hoped that "Soso" would become a great man of the world in the future.

Stalin's future was deeply influenced by his mother. His father was just a clumsy shoemaker, but his mother was an extraordinary woman. She possessed extremely strong perseverance, and she was determined that her son would take the position of pastor in the future.

Stalin's infancy was spent in the village of Gori. Gori is the capital of Georgia and also a place with beautiful scenery. Its secondary school was top-ranked in the area, so it can also be called an educational center.

The Russo-Turkish War had just ended a year before "Soso" was born. When Russian Tsar Alexander II was assassinated in Saint Petersburg, Soso was only fifteen months old. While the Caucasus Mountains echoed with the call for a joint Turkish rebellion against Russia, Soso was still a helpless infant.

Ekaterina often praised her own child. Stalin had excellent grades in school, and his attitude was also very good, so he was quite loved by his teachers. But his body was not very strong, and his family had always been poor, without sufficient food to nourish him. He had smallpox once at the age of seven. Even now, there are still some traces on his face!

"Soso is really a good child," his mother later often solemnly stated, "I never have to punish him. He studies very hard... Soso is my only son, no wonder I love him so much. His father only hoped that he would become a good shoemaker, but Soso also passed away when he was eleven years old. What about me? I don't want Soso to be a shoemaker, but I hope he will be a pastor!"

Stalin received a scholarship when he graduated from elementary school. His early life was undoubtedly frugal. After his father passed away, his mother relied on sewing to barely make a living, and she also saved some money to pay for Soso's education. But this Soso has not disappointed his loving mother's expectations and hard work!

Supplement to the Shen Bao Local Edition Movie Special Issue

The Miserable Situation of a Hollywood Extra 293

— Xuemei

Outside the gate of the film studio stood a crowd of people, men, women, old and young. Among them were former actors from vaudeville troupes, former jockeys, failed entrepreneurs, Chinese girls, ruined millionaires, beggars, etc., but the most heartbroken were the former movie stars and comedians, eliminated by the changing trends of the film industry. They all waited with anticipation, hoping that the gate of the film studio would open its mouth and swallow them all in. "How's your luck?" someone asked a gaunt young woman. She smiled and said, "I've only worked one day in the last seven months. But I'm used to being hungry. Look at that man in the blue velvet vest. I'm much better off than him. I remember he used to be a big manager in a personnel department."

We all know that Hollywood is a dazzling paradise. But in its lower levels, countless wandering souls are seething. They want to break through the golden earth and flood the entire Hollywood with the lava of resentment. There are fifteen thousand extras there, all of whose names are registered with the central personnel employment office. Calling them extras is wronging them, because they may work one day every six months, or never get work at all. They are all hoping—living in hope, eating in hope. But if they are not called extras, or if they do not call themselves extras, they would cut off a line of hope and be unable to endure hunger and cold, waiting for a chance to fall from the sky in the wind and rain. The gates of the film studio are always closed to them. Those who are born in hope will soon die in hope.

How will Hollywood deal with this group of people? Who created this tragedy? It's strange to say. This tragedy was created by the extras themselves. The only way to solve it is to ask the extras themselves to handle it. This group of people, oppressed by economic difficulties and the pain of unemployment, and on the other hand, hearing many rumors of Hollywood's wealth and extravagance, all flocked to Hollywood. When they got there, they registered with the central employment office. Day after day passed. But hope was getting smaller and smaller, the money they brought was gradually running out, they had no food or clothing, and they couldn't pay the rent. But they refused to go elsewhere, still hoping. As for the company, due to economic reasons, it reduced the large scenes in the films, which further reduced the extras' jobs. The following is a tragic scene outside a film studio:

A young extra came out of the casting department of a company, dejected, and mingled with the rest of the extras, lingering and reluctant to leave. "No luck?" someone asked him. He said, "I already got a job, but because I didn't have a pair of glasses, they didn't want me. Buying a pair of glasses costs at least five dollars, where would I get that much money?" He sighed as he spoke. An old man behind him silently took off his glasses and handed them to the young man, saying, "Take them, child. I can't see without glasses, but I can sit here and wait for you." The young man quickly reached out to take the glasses, but when he heard what the old man said, he withdrew his hand and said, "That won't do. You know, once I go in, I might not be able to come out until late at night." The old man said, "It doesn't matter. Take them. Haven't you been hungry for several days? I'll sit at the entrance of that alley and wait for you." The young man thanked him and went in. The old man groped to the entrance of the alley and sat down, unable to move for a day, because he couldn't move an inch without glasses. It was getting late, the sun was setting, and a cold wind was blowing, piercingly cold. Fortunately, the young man came back after eight o'clock. He apologized to the old man, saying, "I'm really sorry. But no matter what, we'll have dinner tonight." He happily put the glasses on the old man and helped him to a nearby restaurant for dinner.

It is a common thing for five or six extras to squeeze into a small room. When the company needs someone, they get busy, your clothes, my shoes, his tie, they put them together and give them to one person, and send him to represent them. When that person comes back from work for a day, everyone has food to eat. The rest, without pants, without clothes, without shoes, sit on the bed and wait. Two beautiful young women even settled down in a cottage in the countryside near Hollywood because they had no place to live. But they are still constantly hoping.

Film Review

Review of "Happiness Ahead" 294

— Ling He

Happiness Ahead

| Da Guangming

This is a timely work. As the New Year is about to come, "Happiness Ahead," which takes the happy New Year as its theme, is being screened in the happy mood of people.

Undoubtedly, this film gives people a full sense of relaxation and pleasure. Such as the New Year's Eve in the dance hall opened by the Chinese, such as in the skating rink, such as when the male protagonist sings while wiping the windows, there is a very good lively atmosphere. This light and lively atmosphere constitutes the main part of the play, and the playwright or director has achieved their goal of making people happy. But we cannot ignore the theme of the work because of these.

What is the theme of the work? In the highly developed capitalist America, it is naturally a very common phenomenon that workers cannot easily marry a rich girl. This phenomenon is not very satisfactory, so he made the rich lady oppose the marriage arranged by her mother, unwilling to marry the young master who is well-matched, and accidentally fall in love with a working youth, a small clerk in a cleaning company. In terms of love, this is what the playwright considers reasonable. But their combination is not without conditions, that is, the male protagonist must have lofty aspirations, strive to climb up from his original position, and start his own cleaning company. He must not take ill-gotten wealth. He must be a gentleman in the eyes of the rich lady. So the lady asked her father to help her lover with a capital of two thousand yuan. After the misunderstanding was explained, the man and woman of two different status were combined.

This play tries its best to cater to the audience's interest in the way of expression, and tries its best to make the plot twists and turns, but it is very far-fetched that the lady refuses to tell her lover her identity, so she rents an apartment, she turns several corners to pay the lover, her father refuses to admit to the male protagonist that he is his father-in-law immediately, these are all for the sake of making a play.

In addition, the actress's acting skills are not mature enough.

Minor Chronicle of "Flying Flower Village" 295

When "Flying Flower Village" went to Linping to shoot on location, Zheng Yingshi was afraid that everyone would be hungry on the way, so he brought a large box of cakes from Shanghai. Unexpectedly, after everyone ate it, they all had intestinal pain, almost causing a disaster. Therefore, when he came back, Zheng Yingshi said to everyone he met, "Damn it, I almost lost my life because of the cake." This is also a strange anecdote in location shooting.

Chen Juanjuan, who plays Xiao Hua, is only six years old this year. But she is very clever and knows ten things from one. When the song "Shepherdess" was recorded, it was highly appreciated by the Western orchestra of Victory Records, who frequently called her "Little Sweetheart".

There is a court scene in the play "Flying Flower Village". In order to make the plot atmosphere realistic, Zheng Yingshi specially rushed to the court to listen to the trial one day. It happened that he was trying a case of seduction, which coincided with the plot in his play. Therefore, the atmosphere of the court scene in "Flying Flower Village" is particularly tense and powerful.

In the recent cold north wind, "Flying Flower Village" once reshot a scene, which was the scene of Gao Zhanfei taking a bath after work. Gao Zhanfei caught a cold because of this, and was in bed for about ten days before getting up.

The most stressful time for "Flying Flower Village" was in the hot summer of June, but the staff of all departments did not stop working because of the hot weather, so there were several cases of heatstroke every day. For example, Qin Tong fainted once and was rushed to the Red Cross for emergency treatment before waking up.

Shi Dongshan completed "Woman" on the day he got a daughter, and the result was indeed beautiful. Zheng Yingshi completed "Flying Flower Village" on the day he got a son, and the result was even more beautiful. Therefore, colleagues who are good at humor, such as Hu Rui, the director of "Elegy of Life", often hold up a stool and shout loudly: "Look at the old man in the sky, bless my old wife who I haven't seen for more than ten years to give birth to a precious son soon, and support my "Elegy of Life"!" Very funny. (But)
