Movie Novel

The Merry Widow (4) 299

— Su Hua

Donald hurriedly replied as if to explain, "Oh! Yes, but it's all too confusing and I can't get rid of it." He stopped suddenly as he said this, and Suria stood up. He also stood up and said, "Do you want me to stay here?" Donald smiled reluctantly, "What are you talking about? Nothing in the world can make me leave you." She continued, "Then I will be confused, maybe I won't be able to get rid of it, what about you?" This stumped Donald. He couldn't say anything. Suria scolded in her heart, "All you need is Fifi, a dancer, you call yourself romantic, but you don't even understand love." Donald couldn't bear it anymore, he pretended to be calm and said, "Please don't ruin tonight?" Suria heard this and said angrily, "Huh, ruin tonight? I won't ruin your tonight, you want your happiness, come here." Saying that, she rushed outside, pointed at Donald and shouted downstairs, "Listen up, this gentleman wants you to accompany him tonight." Then she said to Donald, "They are all here, they are all your tonight. I won't bother you tomorrow." After speaking, she ran downstairs, and finally she said to Donald, "I regret not knowing you were like this sooner." After speaking, she left Maisie. Donald ran to the window and watched her and her car disappear into the night. He was disappointed, and in the room, he drank bottle after bottle of champagne, muttering Fifi's name.

It was the next evening. In Donald's hotel room, Ambassador Buff suddenly arrived and told his servant that if he didn't find Donald and bring him to the embassy immediately, he would be court-martialed. His servant hurriedly took the military uniform and ran to Maisie to find him. The room was full of champagne bottles. He was sleeping soundly. He wouldn't wake up even if you called him. He wanted to close the door and change his clothes for him. After a while, his servant was thrown out, shouting, "He refuses to take off his clothes." The women waiting outside unexpectedly rushed inside. Underwear, outerwear, pants, socks, etc. were all thrown out of the room. Donald was finally dressed in military uniform by this group of people. But he was still drunk, and he was still saying that he would never marry that widow for money. He refused to go to the embassy no matter what. Later, he was pushed and shoved into the car by the women and taken to the embassy. When the car arrived, the embassy was already very chaotic, and the ambassador was anxious and at a loss. As soon as he got out of the car, the ambassador helped him into a small reception room and hurriedly poured coffee into him. He woke up, but still refused to see the widow. The ambassador didn't care about him, went out and brought the widow in to introduce her. After a while, the ambassador came back. He was supporting a noble lady. When Donald saw her, he was stunned. It turned out that the noble lady was the widow, and the widow was Fifi, whom he missed so much. The ambassador introduced them. A triumphant smile appeared on Donald's face, and he leaned down to kiss Suria's weave. She slowly said, "Do you want to take off the veil?" "It's not good, I'm not jumping over the wall." He replied comically. The ambassador standing next to them felt confused when he heard them talking. Donald continued, "Since yesterday, I have been madly in love with a woman, but she left me, her name is Fifi, now only you can help me find her." Suria said with a bitter face, "You should sentence her to death. She left you last night and committed suicide in the hotel." The ambassador was so angry when he heard this that he almost fainted and ran out immediately. They also walked to the garden, and Donald gently said, "I love you so much that it makes me crazy." She replied coldly, "Everyone says they love me, what do they love me for? My beauty? My liveliness? Or my money?" He also replied coldly, "I don't know what others are like, but I am completely for your money." She didn't find it strange. She turned around and used her fan to hit his face. They looked at each other silently, and the music inside sounded. (To be continued)

Home
